(роИ) роЗ%рпЗро▒., роП%? asked the Minister of Rural Economic Affairs:

(a) Will he inform this House-

(i) the number of persons in Sri Lanka who made their livelihood through the curd industry by the end of 2015;

(i) whether the Government has taken steps to increase the buffalo population;

(ii) if so, what those steps are?

(d) If not, why?

(c) If not, why?

[р╢Ь р╢┤р╖Пр╢и┬Я р╢аV р╢Ъ р╢╗р╢лр╖Ар╢Ъ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П]

2017 р╖Щр╢▒Aр╖Ар╖РVр╢╢- 11

asked the Prime Minister and Minister of National Policies and Economic Affairs:

(a) Is he aware that-

(i) the 190 perches land (Deed No. 16) located at No. 11, Station Road, Mannar has been registered (Reg. No. B 1/53) as a land owned by the Methodist Council on 17.12.1872 by the Land Office of Mannar;

(ii) the Sri Lanka Army established an office in the respective land when it was unable to maintain it following the tense situation that prevailed in the country in 1985; and

(iii) even after more than 3 years have passed after allocating a separate land near the Mannar town for the purpose, the Army is yet to release the land belonging to the Methodist Council?

(b) Will he inform this House whether measures will be taken soon to release the relevant land which is urgently required by the Methodist Council?

Eran Wickramaratne) Hon. Member, just to quickly comment on some of the matters that you raised, I want to say that we do not protect any illegal economic activity and certainly, the Hon. Prime Minister will not tolerate any illegal economic activity. We have absolutely no intention of promoting alcohol; particularly in the Northern Province. Our policy is completely neutral. I might also say that we must also defend the right of every investor to go anywhere in this country and invest so that they will create jobs and opportunities for all the people.

We are particularly concerned that after the war, economic activities in the Northern Province have been slow and we want to encourage investors to go there. So, when we brought the Inland Revenue Bill to Parliament, we gave a capital allowance for the country. That is, if you invest Rs. 100, you do not have to pay tax till you get that Rs. 100 back. But, if an investor goes to the North, we give a 200 per cent capital allowance to him. That means, the investors can recover their investments and 100 per cent more of their investments, if they go to North. So, our policy is geographically neutral and we certainly want to strengthen the economy in the Northern Province. р╢Ь, ┬Б2р╢нY р╖Щр╢║@р╖Щр╖Дqр╖Гр╖Кр╖Ар╢╗3 р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛+.рооро┐ роЪрпАройро┐/род"рокро┐ рпЗропро╛рпЗроХIро╡ро░) (The Hon. Xро▒ро┐рпЖроХро╛5ро│ ро╡ро┐FроХро┐%рпЗро▒%. р╢Ь, р╢Йр╢╗р╖П3 -fр╢╕р╢╗.р╢▒ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П ( р╢п р╢╗р╖Пр╢вA р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нA+р╢╕р╖П) (рооро╛+.рооро┐ роЗро░ро╛ ро╡ро┐роХро┐ро░рооро░/рой - роиро┐родро┐ роЗро░ро╛роЬро╛роХ роЕрпИроо!роЪ5) The Hon. Eran Wickramaratne - State Minister of Finance) Thank you for the points that are being made. I just want to quickly point out that out of the 116 lagoons, we are going to invest in ten this year for which we have allocated Rs. 1,000 million. We are going to cover the following lagoons: namely, Batticaloa, Nandikadal and Nayaru. In addition to that, we are also basically desilting the lagoons in the Northern Province. We are also going to allow multi-day boats and have allocated a lot of money - about Rs. 400 million - for that. Part of it is going to the North. We want to make sure that it will happen.

As stated under No.60 of the Budget Speech, we will develop and upgrade the anchorages and landing sites of fisheries locations also. In addition to Chilaw and Mirissa fishery harbours, we are going to improve the Karainagar fishery harbour as well.

I would also like to point out that the good thing in allocating money is, we have named the places this time, so that you could monitor the progress of how the Budget allocation will be handled.

As stated under No. 265 of the Budget Speech, we will strengthen reconciliation focused on livelihood development. We understand the problem particularly of the women-headed households in the North. There are some of the financial problems caused through the microfinance institutions and so forth. We cannot really directly intervene with them because these are non-governmental organizations. But, this is done through the Government; we have allocated Rs. 2,750 million on economic empowerment and also to build social infrastructure. We will also build a special home for differently abled women in the North; we have allocated money for that too.

As stated under No. 269 of the Budget Speech, the Government will support, by way of grants, selected small industries throughout the Northern Province by empowering the vast network of Producer Cooperatives in

the Province. That is only for the Northern Province and for that we have again allocated Rs. 1,000 million.

As stated under No. 272 of the Budget Speech, only about 50 per cent of the Achchuveli Industrial Zone is utilized at present and we propose to bear 50 per cent of the electricity cost as an incentive and if companies go and establish themselves there and we have allocated money for that.

As I said in the morning as well, in the Inland Revenue Bill, we have made a special mention that we give a 100 per cent capital allowance for anybody investing in addition to the regular depreciation. If they invest in the Northern Province, we have made an exception by giving them a 200 per cent capital allowance.

Thank you. р╢Ь, р╢ер╖Пр╢▒ .+ ┬Ыр╖Щ3р╖Г3 р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛+.рооро┐ роЮро╛рой0/ VрпЗроироЪ) (The Hon. Gnanamuthu Srineshan) Thank you.

р╖Щр╢╕e ┬лfр╢Ъ |р╢Ъ р╢Йр╢ВD р╢╖р╖Пр╖Вр╖Пр╖Щр╖А1 )р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щ1. р╢╕р╢╕ р╢Ср╢║ р╢║р╖А1р╢▒V. тАЬThe science is clear: A childтАЩs brain is built, not born.тАЭ

р╖Щр╢╕e )р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒ р╢Кр╖Ер╢Я р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢лр╢║+ р╢╕р╢╕ р╢║р╖А1р╢▒V.

тАЬThe early moments of life offer an unparalleled opportunity to build the brains of the children who will ultimately build the future.

But far too often, this is an opportunity squandered.

For nations, the cost of not investing in a childтАЩs early moments is a generation with poorer health, fewer learning skills and reduced earning potential. It is a weaker economy and a greater burden on health, education and welfare systems. It is intergenerational cycles of poverty and disadvantage that hinder equitable growth and prosperity. For children, especially children from disadvantaged communities, the price of this failure is lost potential.тАЭ

тАЬCurrently, Sri Lanka invests only 0.0001 per cent of its gross domestic product (GDP) on early childhood programmes. This is one of the lowest ratios of public spending on early childhood development in the world; lower than its South Asian neighbors but lower even than many very poor Sub-Saharan African countries.тАЭ

р╖ЩV р╖Ар╢▒ р╢з р╢Ьр╖Пр╢╜ р╖Гр╖К┬ЬYр╢Ър╖ЩJ р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢╢р╢╜р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒ *р╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢╕ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢з├Бр╖АY р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢┤+ р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П )р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П, р╢Ер╖Щ┬Ш р╖Гр╖К┬ЬYр╢Ър╖ЩJ р╖Ар╖Рf р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢ЬV D1 р╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒р╢║ р╢Ър╢╗0 р╢╜р╢╢р╢▒ р╖А$ р╢Жр╢нр╖А р╢╢┬Ър╢╜ р╖Щр╢╜р╖Г р╢Ъ┬Щ р╖Щр╢┤A р╖Ар╢Ьр╖П р╢Ър╢╗1р╢▒ ┬Зр╢пр╖Пр╢▒V р╢╕. р╢Е р╖ЩVр╢Ъ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╖Щр╖ГAр╢║р╖П р╢╢р╢╜р╖П р╖Гр╖К┬ЬY р╖ГVр╢╢1Xр╢Ър╢╗р╢л р╢ЪB┬Щр╖Щ6 р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╖Ер╖Пр╢╕ р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢╜р╖РrU р╢Л+р╢нр╢╗р╢║ р╢нр╢╕N р╖Щр╖ДYр╖Щр╢зр╢║р╖Пр╢╗ Dр╢пр╖Др╖Гр╢Ъ р╖Ар╢Ьр╖П р╢Ър╢╗1р╢▒ р╢Е0р╢╕р╖Р)р╢║ {р╢╜р╖П )р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖ПN р╢║р╢▒ р╢Ср╢Ъ. р╢▒@+, р╢Ер╖Щ┬Ш р╖Гр╖К┬ЬYр╢Ър╖ЩJр╢╕ р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╢з р╖Щр╖ДYр╖Щр╢зр╢║р╖Пр╢╗ р╢пр╖Д р╢┤р╖Др╖Щр╖ЕAр╖Гр╖К р╢пр╖Др╖Гр╢Ъ р╢Ъ┬Щр╖Щр╢┤A р╖Ар╢Ьр╖П р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Г1. р╢Ъ┬Щр╖Щр╢┤A р╢║р╢▒ р╖Щр╢╖р╢Ьр╢║ р╢Ер╖Щ┬Ш р╢╕р╖Др╖Щр╢┤Aр╖Щр╖ЕAр╖Ар╢з р╢Ьр╖Рр╖Ер╖Щр╢┤р╢▒ р╖Щр╢╖р╢Ьр╢║Y р╢║р╢╜р╖П р╢╕р╖П р╖Бр╖Кр╖Ар╖Пр╖Г р╢Ър╢╗1р╖Щ1 р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. р╢Т р╢нр╢╗Y р╖Щр╢▒Aр╖Щр╖АN. р╖Ар╖Рf р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢ЬVр╖Аf1 р╖Щр╖Г р╖Ар╢Ьр╖Пр╖А1р╢з р╢пр╢╗р╢▒ р╢║р╢пр╢╕р╢з р╖Гр╖Пр╖Щ┬ШYр╖Вр╖А р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ р╖Ар╢Ьр╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╢пр╢╗р╢▒ р╢║р╢пр╢╕ р╢Е3 ┬ир╢л+, р╢Ф┬и1р╢з р╢╜р╖Пр╢╖р╢║Y )rр╢л+ р╢┤р╖ПGр╖ГGр╢Ъ р╖Ар╖Бр╖Щр╢║0+, р╢Ер╖Щ┬Ш *р╖ЩEр╖Бр╖ЩJ ┬жр╖А+р╖Ар╢▒ р╢ЪVр╢Ъ р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╖Щ┬Ы р╢Ж-.р╢Ър╢║ р╢┤р╖Р+р╖Щр╢н0+ р╢Ь+р╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╖ЩV р╖Щр╢╖р╢Ьр╢║ р╢Ер╖Щ┬Ш р╢┤р╖Ер╖П+р╖Ар╢╜р╢з р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╢Еeр╢нр╢Ър╢╗ р╖Щр╢╖р╢Ьр╢║Y.

┬лр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П├║р╢к р╢Ь р╢╕1┬о$р╢╕ , р╢Ер╖Щ┬Ш *р╖ЩEр╖Бр╖Ар╢╜ р╖А$ р╢Жр╢нр╖А р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╢пр╖П )rU vр╢Вp vр╢Вp р╢Зр╖Е р╢╕р╖П-р╢Ь, р╖Щр╢пAр╖Е р╢╕р╖П-р╢Ь Dр╢║р╢╜ р╖ЩV р╖Ар╢▒ р╢з D├Э р╖Щр╢ЬAр╖Гр╖К )р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢нр╖А+ р╢Е┬и l 7Y, 8Y, 10Y р╢║р╢▒р╖Щр╢ЪAр╢з р╢Ер╖Щ┬Ш р╖Гр╖К┬ЬYр╢Ър╢║ р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ р╢┤р╖П┬Ср╢║ р╢вр╢╜ р╢Е-rр╢пр╢║р╢Ър╢з @┬Ър╢л р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Фр╢╢$р╢╕р╖П р╖Щр╢║р╢вр╢▒р╢║ р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╖Щр╢╕Aр╢▒р╢╗р╖Пр╢Ьр╢╜ р╖Гр╖К┬ЬYр╢Ър╖ЩJ р╢Зр╢нр╖РV *р╖ЩEр╖Бр╖Ар╢╜ р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖А @┬Ър╢л р╖Щр╢пр╢▒ р╢┤р╖П┬Ср╢║ р╢вр╢╜ *р╖Бр╖Кр╢▒р╢║р╢Ър╢з р╢Ер╢┤р╢з+ р╖Ар╖Р┬г р╢Ъ р╖Щр╢▒Aр╖Щр╢ЬAр╖Гр╖К @┬Ър╢л р╖Щр╢п1р╢▒ Dl р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ъ┬Щ р╖Щр╢┤A р╖Ар╢Ьр╖Пр╖А р╢Тр╢Ър╢з р╢Ср╢Ър╢╕ р╖Щр╖Дy$р╖А N р╢║р╢╜р╖П р╢╕р╖П р╢║1р╖Щ1 р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. р╢▒@+, р╢Ср╢║ р╢Ср╢Ъ *р╢░р╖Пр╢▒ р╖Щр╖Дy$р╖АY р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢┤+ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П.
